[COMPONENTS]
@C1
assay: TEXT | An assay based on 10X Genomics. Example : 100x3’ v2
assay_ontology_term_id: TEXT | Experimental Factor Ontology ID (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/efo)
cell_type_ontology_term_id: TEXT | Cell Ontology ID (i.e. CL:0000784)  (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/cl)
development_stage: TEXT | Human development stage derived from HsapDv term  (Example if data is Homo sapiens, development stage is obtained from Link. HsapDv:0000114 - 20-year-old human stage)
development_stage_ontology_term_id: TEXT | Human Developmental Stages ID (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/hsapdv) or Mouse Developmental Stages ID (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/mmusdv) (HsapDv if human, MmusDv if mouse, unknown if information unavailable)
disease: TEXT | Description of disease (example: lung adenocarcinoma) or normal cells
disease_ontology_term_id: TEXT | MONDO disease ontology ID (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/mondo) (ex. MONDO:0100426 or PATO:0000461 for 'normal')
donor_id: TEXT | Identifies a unique individual that data were derived from
feature_biotype: TEXT | Biological type of feature (e.g. gene)
feature_is_filtered: BOOLEAN | Indicates if the feature (gene) was/should be filtered in analysis
feature_name: TEXT | Gene name from HUGO Human Gene Nomenclature Committee (https://www.genenames.org/)
feature_reference: TEXT | A reference to the feature: NCBI Taxonomy ID
is_primary_data: BOOLEAN | Indicates if the sample is primary or not (True/False)
organism: TEXT | The genus and species from which biosamples are derived
organism_ontology_term_id: TEXT | NCBITaxon ID (REF: https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/taxonomy) (ex. NCBITaxon:9606 for human, NCBITaxon:10090 for mouse)
self_reported_ethnicity: TEXT | Ethnicity of the individual (obtained from HANCESTRO terms for Homo sapiens)
self_reported_ethnicity_ontology_term_id: TEXT | If human, the Human Ancestry Ontology ID (i.e. HANCESTRO:0005) (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/hancestro); "multiethnic" if more than one ethnicity. "Unknown" if human and no information, else "na" if non-human
sex: TEXT | Phenotypic sex
sex_ontology_term_id: TEXT | Phenotype And Trait Ontology ID, PATO:0000384 for male, PATO:0000383 for female, or unknown if unavailable
suspension_type: TEXT | Cell, nucleus, or na, as corresponding to sample preparation
tissue_ontology_term_id: TEXT | Uber-anatomy ontology ID (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/uberon) (ex.UBERON:2001190)

@C2
AJCC_Clinical_M: TEXT | Extent of the distant metastasis for the cancer based on evidence obtained from clinical
 assessment parameters determined prior to treatment.
AJCC_Clinical_N: TEXT | Extent of the regional lymph node involvement for the cancer based on evidence obtained from
 clinical assessment parameters determined prior to treatment.
AJCC_Clinical_Stage: TEXT | Stage group determined from clinical information on the tumor (T), regional node (N) and
 metastases (M) and by grouping cases with similar prognosis for cancer.
AJCC_Clinical_T: TEXT | Extent of the primary cancer based on evidence obtained from clinical assessment parameters
 determined prior to treatment.
AJCC_Pathologic_M: TEXT | Code to represent the defined absence or presence of distant spread or metastases (M) to
 locations via vascular channels or lymphatics beyond the regional lymph nodes, using
 criteria established by the American Joint Committee on Cancer (AJCC).
AJCC_Pathologic_N: TEXT | The codes that represent the stage of cancer based on the nodes present (N stage) according
 to criteria based on multiple editions of the AJCC's Cancer Staging Manual.
AJCC_Pathologic_Stage: TEXT | The extent of a cancer, especially whether the disease has spread from the original site to
 other parts of the body based on AJCC staging criteria.
AJCC_Pathologic_T: TEXT | Code of pathological T (primary tumor) to define the size or contiguous extension of the
 primary tumor (T), using staging criteria from the American Joint Committee on Cancer
 (AJCC).
AJCC_Staging_System_Edition: TEXT | The text term used to describe the version or edition of the American Joint Committee on Cancer
 Staging Handbooks, a publication by the group formed for the purpose of developing a system of
 staging for cancer that is acceptable to the American medical profession and is compatible with
 other accepted classifications.
Anaplasia_Present: TEXT | Yes/no/unknown/Not Reported indicator used to describe whether anaplasia was present at the
time of diagnosis.
Anaplasia_Present_Type: TEXT | The text term used to describe the morphologic findings indicating the presence of a malignant cellular infiltrate characterized by the presence of large pleomorphic cells, necrosis, and high mitotic activity in a tissue sample.
Best_Overall_Response: TEXT | The best improvement achieved throughout the entire course of protocol treatment.
Breslow_Thickness: TEXT | The number that describes the distance, in millimeters, between the upper layer of the epidermis and the deepest point of tumor penetration.
Classification_of_Tumor: TEXT | Text that describes the kind of disease present in the tumor specimen as related to a specific timepoint.
Cog_Neuroblastoma_Risk_Group: TEXT | Text term that represents the categorization of patients on the basis of prognostic factors per a system developed by Children's Oncology Group (COG). Risk level is used to assign treatment intensity.
Cog_Rhabdomyosarcoma_Risk_Group: TEXT | Text term used to describe the classification of rhabdomyosarcoma, as defined by the Children's Oncology Group (COG).
Days_to_Diagnosis: TEXT | Number of days between the date used for index and the date the patient was diagnosed with the malignant disease.
First_Symptom_Prior_to_Diagnosis: TEXT | Text term used to describe the patient's first symptom experienced prior to diagnosis and thought to be related to the disease.
Gleason_Grade_Group: TEXT | The text term used to describe the overall grouping of grades defined by the Gleason grading classification, which is used to determine the aggressiveness of prostate cancer. Note that this grade describes the entire prostatectomy specimen and is not specific to the sample used for sequencing.
Gleason_Grade_Tertiary: TEXT | The text term used to describe the tertiary pattern as described by the Gleason Grading System.
Gleason_Patterns_Percent: TEXT | Numeric value that represents the percentage of Patterns 4 and 5, which is used when the Gleason score is greater than 7 to predict prognosis.
Greatest_Tumor_Dimension: TEXT | Numeric value that represents the measurement of the widest portion of the tumor in centimeters.
Gross_Tumor_Weight: TEXT | Numeric value used to describe the gross pathologic tumor weight, measured in grams.
IGCCCG_Stage: TEXT | The text term used to describe the International Germ Cell Cancer Collaborative Group (IGCCCG), a grouping used to further classify metastatic testicular tumors.
INPC_Grade: TEXT | Text term used to describe the classification of neuroblastic differentiation within neuroblastoma tumors, as defined by the International Neuroblastoma Pathology Classification (INPC).
INPC_Histologic_Group: TEXT | The text term used to describe the classification of neuroblastomas distinguishing between favorable and unfavorable histologic groups. The histologic score, defined by the International Neuroblastoma Pathology Classification (INPC), is based on age, mitosis-karyorrhexis index (MKI), stromal content and degree of tumor cell differentiation.
INRG_Stage: TEXT | The text term used to describe the staging classification of neuroblastic tumors, as defined by the International Neuroblastoma Risk Group (INRG).
INSS_Stage: TEXT | Text term used to describe the staging classification of neuroblastic tumors, as defined by the International Neuroblastoma Staging System (INSS).
International_Prognostic_Index: TEXT | The text term used to describe the International Prognostic Index, which classifies the prognosis of patients with aggressive non-Hodgkin's lymphoma.
IRS_Group: TEXT | Text term used to describe the classification of rhabdomyosarcoma tumors, as defined by the Intergroup Rhabdomyosarcoma Study (IRS).
IRS_Stage: TEXT | The text term used to describe the classification of rhabdomyosarcoma tumors, as defined by the Intergroup Rhabdomyosarcoma Study (IRS).
ISS_Stage: TEXT | The multiple myeloma disease stage at diagnosis.
Laterality: TEXT | For tumors in paired organs, designates the side on which the cancer originates.
Lymph_Node_Involved_Site: TEXT | The text term used to describe the anatomic site of lymph node involvement.
Lymph_Nodes_Positive: TEXT | The number of lymph nodes involved with disease as determined by pathologic examination.
Lymph_Nodes_Tested: TEXT | The number of lymph nodes tested to determine whether lymph nodes were involved with disease as determined by a pathologic examination.
Lymphatic_Invasion_Present: TEXT | A yes/no indicator to ask if small or thin-walled vessel invasion is present, indicating lymphatic involvement
Margin_Distance: TEXT | Numeric value (in centimeters) that represents the distance between the tumor and the surgical margin.
Margins_Involved_Site: TEXT | The text term used to describe the anatomic sites that were involved in the survival margins.
Medulloblastoma_Molecular_Classification: TEXT | The text term used to describe the classification of medulloblastoma tumors based on molecular features.
Metastasis_at_Diagnosis: TEXT | The text term used to describe the extent of metastatic disease present at diagnosis.
Metastasis_at_Diagnosis_Site: TEXT | Text term to identify an anatomic site in which metastatic disease involvement is found.
Method_of_Diagnosis: TEXT | Text term used to describe the method used to confirm the patients malignant diagnosis.
Micropapillary_Features: TEXT | The yes/no/unknown indicator used to describe whether micropapillary features were determined to be present.
Mitosis_Karyorrhexis_Index: TEXT | Text term that represents the component of the International Neuroblastoma Pathology Classification (INPC) for mitosis-karyorrhexis index (MKI).
Mitotic_Count: TEXT | The number of mitoses identified under the microscope in tumors. The method of counting varies, according to the specific tumor examined. Usually, the mitotic count is determined based on the number of mitoses per high power field (40X) or 10 high power fields.
Non_Nodal_Regional_Disease: TEXT | The text term used to describe whether the patient had non-nodal regional disease.
Non_Nodal_Tumor_Deposits: TEXT | The yes/no/unknown indicator used to describe the presence of tumor deposits in the pericolic or perirectal fat or in adjacent mesentery away from the leading edge of the tumor.
Ovarian_Specimen_Status: TEXT | The text term used to describe the physical condition of the involved ovary.
Ovarian_Surface_Involvement: TEXT | The text term that describes whether the surface tissue (outer boundary) of the ovary shows evidence of involvement or presence of cancer.
Percent_Tumor_Invasion: TEXT | The percentage of tumor cells spread locally in a malignant neoplasm through infiltration or destruction of adjacent tissue.
Perineural_Invasion_Present: TEXT | A yes/no indicator to ask if perineural invasion or infiltration of tumor or cancer is present.
Peritoneal_Fluid_Cytological_Status: TEXT | The text term used to describe the malignant status of the peritoneal fluid determined by cytologic testing.
Pregnant_at_Diagnosis: TEXT | The text term used to indicate whether the patient was pregnant at the time they were diagnosed.
Primary_Gleason_Grade: TEXT | The text term used to describe the primary Gleason score, which describes the pattern of cells making up the largest area of the tumor. The primary and secondary Gleason pattern grades are combined to determine the patient's Gleason grade group, which is used to determine the aggresiveness of prostate cancer. Note that this grade describes the entire prostatectomy specimen and is not specific to the sample used for sequencing.
Prior_Malignancy: TEXT | The yes/no/unknown indicator used to describe the patient's history of prior cancer diagnosis.
Prior_Treatment: TEXT | A yes/no/unknown/not applicable indicator related to the administration of therapeutic agents received before the body specimen was collected.
Residual_Disease: TEXT | Text terms to describe the status of a tissue margin following surgical resection.
Secondary_Gleason_Grade: TEXT | The text term used to describe the secondary Gleason score, which describes the pattern of cells making up the second largest area of the tumor. The primary and secondary Gleason pattern grades are combined to determine the patient's Gleason grade group, which is used to determine the aggresiveness of prostate cancer. Note that this grade describes the entire prostatectomy specimen and is not specific to the sample used for sequencing.
Supratentorial_Localization: TEXT | Text term to specify the location of the supratentorial tumor.
Synchronous_Malignancy: TEXT | A yes/no/unknown indicator used to describe whether the patient had an additional malignant diagnosis at the same time the tumor used for sequencing was diagnosed. If both tumors were sequenced, both tumors would have synchronous malignancies.
Tumor_Confined_to_Organ_of_Origin: TEXT | The yes/no/unknown indicator used to describe whether the tumor is confined to the organ where it originated and did not spread to a proximal or distant location within the body.
Tumor_Depth: TEXT | Numeric value that represents the depth of tumor invasion, measured in millimeters (mm).
Tumor_Focality: TEXT | The text term used to describe whether the patient's disease originated in a single location or multiple locations.
Vascular_Invasion_Present: TEXT | The yes/no indicator to ask if large vessel or venous invasion was detected by surgery or presence in a tumor specimen.
Vascular_Invasion_Type: TEXT | Text term that represents the type of vascular tumor invasion.
WHO_CNS_Grade: TEXT | WHO CNS Grade
WHO_NTE_Grade: TEXT | WHO NTE Grade
Year_of_Diagnosis: TEXT | Numeric value to represent the year of an individual's initial pathologic diagnosis of cancer.

AA_Change: TEXT | Alphanumeric value used to describe the amino acid change for a specific genetic variant. Example: R116Q. Note: This node is meant to capture molecular tests that were completed clinically for the participant and only includes data from diagnostic array that was completed prior to research sequencing was done. Do not include data related to research assay outputs here.
Antigen: TEXT | The text term used to describe an antigen included in molecular testing. Note: This node is meant to capture molecular tests that were completed clinically for the participant and only includes data from diagnostic array that was completed prior to research sequencing was done. Do not include data related to research assay outputs here.

Note: This node is meant to capture molecular tests that were completed clinically for the participant and only includes data from diagnostic array that was completed prior to research sequencing was done. Do not include data related to research assay outputs here.

If a specific genetic variant is being reported, this property can be used to capture the chromosome where that variant is located. Note: This node is meant to capture molecular tests that were completed clinically for the participant and only includes data from diagnostic array that was completed prior to research sequencing was done. Do not include data related to research assay outputs here.

Do not include data related to research assay outputs here.

Do not include data related to research assay outputs here.

If a specific genetic variant is being reported, this property can be used to capture the cytoband where the variant is located. Format: [chromosome][chromosome arm].[band+sub-bands]. Example: 17p13.1. Note: This node is meant to capture molecular tests that were completed clinically for the participant and only includes data from diagnostic array that was completed prior to research sequencing was done. Intron: TEXT | Intron number targeted or included in molecular analysis. If a specific genetic variant is being reported, this property can be used to capture the intron where that variant is located.

Second_Exon: TEXT | The second exon number involved in molecular variation. If a specific genetic variant is being reported, this property can be used to capture the second exon where that variant is located. Parent: TEXT | Parent class of this attribute - i.e. where to "hook" this attribute into an existing schema. Note that this assumes a single existing schema/a single json-ld schema context; if we need to support classes/attributes/properties defined across multiple schemas/json-ld contexts we'd need to add a schema/context column that specifies the context of each attribute, if different from the context of the attribute's parent.
Properties: TEXT | Properties specific to a particular attribute; note that properties could be attributes themselves (i.e. listed under the "Attributes" column).
Required: TEXT | Indicate if specifying value for attribute X is mandatory or optional by default. Set to TRUE or FALSE. If TRUE, a data contributor must provide a value for attribute X (e.g. one of the valid values in 'Valid Values', if any are specified). If FALSE, a data contributor may select between 'Not Applicable' or 'Not Specified' as a value for attribute X. Note that an attribute may not be required by default (i.e. 'Required' is set to FALSE), but it could be required by virtue of being an attribute of another required attribute (e.g. see ERCC).
Source: TEXT | The source for the description of the term, usually an URI. Ontologies can be used as sources. E.g. Library Construction Method has source: http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/OBI_0000711
Valid_Values: TEXT | The range of attribute X: the values that can be assigned to attribute X; these values can include/be other attributes (i.e. listed in the 'Attribute' columns) themselves. Comma separated. If none provided any non-null value is valid for attribute X.
Validation_Rules: TEXT | What type of data is allowed in the Valid Values column. Only relevant if Valid Values are not present in the row. E.g. string, list, integer

An ellipse whose eccentricity is 0 is actually a circle, while an ellipse whose eccentricity is 1 is a line segment.)
